[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `exif_get_slong` in `[0m[35m/src/libexif/libexif/[0m[95mexif-utils.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m137:36[0m[39m` - Where the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mactual overflow occurs[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Overflow Location**: The overflow occurs at line [0m[1;36m137[0m[39m, column [0m[1;36m36[0m[39m in [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif-utils.c` within the `exif_get_slong` function, which is called by [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_get_long`.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Memory Layout**: The shadow bytes reveal that the accessed memory location is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min a heap redzone area [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmarked as `fa`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating it's outside the bounds of the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated buffer but within the padding area added by AddressSanitizer for [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetection purposes.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Fuji Makernote Specific**: The vulnerability is triggered specifically when [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing Fuji camera makernote data, as evidenced by the call to [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_mnote_data_fuji_load`.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Data Reading Pattern**: The issue involves reading integer values [0m[1;39m([0m[39msigned long[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor long[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m from the EXIF data stream, suggesting insufficient boundary validation [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen parsing multi-byte values.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Check for integer overflow using subtraction pattern[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m This prevents: datao + offset_to_entries > buf_size[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdatao > buf_size - offset_to_entries[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    exif_log [0m[1;39m([0m[39men->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataFuji"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Entry offset out of bounds [0m[32m([0m[32m%u + %u > %u[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m,[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned int[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mdatao, offset_to_entries, buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Step [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m: Safe to perform the addition[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdatao += offset_to_entries;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Step [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m: Verify we have space for the entry count [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mCHECKOVERFLOW[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdatao, buf_size, [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. **Secondary Fix: Validate Entry Data Offsets** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mHigh Priority[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `libexif/fuji/exif-mnote-data-fuji.[0m[1;92mc:244[0m[39m`[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApply the same validation pattern:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Original code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m244[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdataofs = exif_get_long [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + dataofs, n->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + n->offset;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m New safe implementation:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mExifLong data_offset = exif_get_long [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + dataofs, n->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Validate the offset value[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata_offset > buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    exif_log [0m[1;39m([0m[39men->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataFuji"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Invalid data offset in entry"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    continue;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Check for overflow in the addition [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + n->offset + data_offset[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize_t base_offset = [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + n->offset;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbase_offset > buf_size || data_offset > buf_size - base_offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    exif_log [0m[1;39m([0m[39men->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataFuji"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Data offset out of bounds"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    continue;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdataofs = data_offset + base_offset;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. **Enhanced Boundary Validation** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSupporting Fix[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Additional check at line [0m[1;36m166[0m[39m**: The current check validates header size, but we [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould also ensure the read position for the offset is valid:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m After line [0m[1;36m171[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdatao = [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + n->offset;[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mCHECKOVERFLOW[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdatao, buf_size, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    exif_log [0m[1;39m([0m[39men->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataFuji"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Cannot read MakerNote header offset"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis ensures we can safely read [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mto get to the offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m plus [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset value itself[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. **Infrastructure Enhancement for Future-Proofing** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional but [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRecommended[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo properly track MakerNote size throughout the codebase:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**In `exif-data.[0m[1;92mc:55[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m71[0m[39m`**, add a size field to `_ExifDataPrivate`:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstruct _ExifDataPrivate[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    ExifByteOrder order;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    ExifMnoteData *md;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    ExifLog *log;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    ExifMem *mem;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    unsigned int ref_count;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Temporarily used while loading data *[0m[35m/[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    unsigned int offset_mnote;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    unsigned int size_mnote;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m ADD THIS[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    ExifDataOption options;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    ExifDataType data_type;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m[39m;[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**In `exif-data.[0m[1;92mc:233[0m[39m`**, store the size:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata->priv->offset_mnote = doff;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata->priv->size_mnote = s;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m ADD THIS[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Add a new method in `exif-mnote-data-priv.h:[0m[1;36m44[0m[39m`**:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvoid [0m[1;39m([0m[39m* set_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExifMnoteData *, unsigned int[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**In `exif-data.[0m[1;92mc:836[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m838[0m[39m`**, pass the size:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexif_mnote_data_set_offset [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata->priv->md, data->priv->offset_mnote[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexif_mnote_data_set_size [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata->priv->md, data->priv->size_mnote[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m ADD THIS[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexif_mnote_data_load [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata->priv->md, d, ds[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**In `exif-mnote-data-fuji.h:[0m[1;36m31[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m39[0m[39m`**, add size to the structure:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstruct _ExifMnoteDataFuji [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    ExifMnoteData parent;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    MnoteFujiEntry *entries;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    unsigned int count;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    ExifByteOrder order;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    unsigned int offset;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    unsigned int max_size;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m ADD THIS[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m[39m;[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThen implement `[0m[1;35mexif_mnote_data_fuji_set_size[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and use `n->max_size` for [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation instead of `buf_size`.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Addresses Root Cause**: The fix directly addresses the lack of validation [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore using untrusted offset values[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Prevents Integer Overflow**: Using the subtraction pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`a > max - b`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstead of addition [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`a + b > max`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m prevents integer overflow vulnerabilities[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Follows Established Patterns**: The fix mirrors the validation pattern used in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_data_load_data_entry` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m192[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m208[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which is the correct reference [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation in the codebase[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Minimal Changes**: The primary fix requires changes only in the Fuji loader [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout modifying the public API or other modules[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Comprehensive**: Addresses both the primary vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m175[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msimilar patterns [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m244[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **No Functional Changes**: The fix only adds validation; it doesn't change how [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalid data is processed[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Same Data Flow**: The loader still receives the full buffer and offset, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaintaining compatibility[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Consistent Error Handling**: Uses existing `exif_log` and early return [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatterns[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Backward Compatible**: Valid EXIF files will continue to work exactly as [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Evaluation Report[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Heap Buffer Overflow**: The validation prevents reading beyond allocated [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundaries by checking offsets before use[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Scariness Score [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m**: Reduces risk by preventing out-of-bounds reads [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompletely[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Fuji Makernote Specific**: Directly fixes the vulnerable code path identified [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the call stack[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **AddressSanitizer Detection**: The fix prevents the [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte overflow that [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered ASAN by ensuring all reads stay within bounds[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Malformed Files Rejected**: Files with intentionally or accidentally malformed[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMakerNote data will be rejected[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is desirable behavior; the loader logs clear error [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmessages indicating the problem[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Performance**: Adds minimal validation overhead [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma few integer comparisons[0m[1;39m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: The cost is negligible compared to the memory operations that [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollow[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Similar Issues in Other Loaders**: The Olympus loader has the same [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability pattern[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: The same fix pattern should be applied to other makernote [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloaders [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOlympus line [0m[1;36m385[0m[39m, and entry data offset reads in all loaders[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Reference to Similar Solutions[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix directly follows the pattern used in `[0m[1;35mexif_data_load_data_entry[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at lines[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m192[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m208[0m[39m in `exif-data.c`, which correctly validates offsets:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdoff = exif_get_long [0m[1;39m([0m[39md + offset + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, data->priv->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdoff >= size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39ms > size - doff[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith the codebase architecture.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
